        <span style="font-family: 宋体; background-color: inherit;">当选择了版本和下载方式（二进制</span><span lang="EN-US" style="background-color: inherit;">tar</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; background-color: inherit;">包）后，下方显示了不止一个对应的</span><span lang="EN-US" style="background-color: inherit;">tar</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; background-color: inherit;">包，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; background-color: inherit;">他们的区别如下：（官方文档里有解释）</span>
    • ssl100 - for all Debian/Ubuntu versions (libssl.so.1.0.0&nbsp;=&gt;&nbsp;/usr/lib/x86_64-linux-gnu/libssl.so.1.0.0&nbsp;(0x00007f2e389a5000));

    • ssl101 - for CentOS 6 and CentOS 7 (libssl.so.10&nbsp;=&gt;&nbsp;/usr/lib64/libssl.so.10(0x00007facbe8c4000));

          <span style="color: red; font-family: 宋体; background-color: inherit;">此处选择</span><span style="color: red; font-family: 宋体; background-color: inherit;">下载</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color: red; background-color: inherit;">ssl101</span><span style="color: red; font-family: 宋体; background-color: inherit;">对应的</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color: red; background-color: inherit;">tar</span><span style="color: red; font-family: 宋体; background-color: inherit;">包</span>

<div style="font: 14px/21px 微软雅黑; text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); text-transform: none; text-indent: 0px; letter-spacing: normal; word-spacing: 0px; white-space: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">

        <font color="#ff0000" face="宋体" style="background-color: inherit;">自定义安装目录是/data</font>

        <font color="#ff0000" face="宋体" style="background-color: inherit;">cd /data</font>

    <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 微软雅黑; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">

            groupadd mysql

            useradd -r -g mysql mysql

            mkdir -p /data/mysql/data/

            mkdir -p /data/mysql/log/

            chown -R mysql.mysql&nbsp; /data/mysql/

        <div style="background-color: inherit;">
            <span lang="EN-US" style="background-color: inherit;">#</span><span style="background-color: inherit;">默认读取<span lang="EN-US" style="background-color: inherit;">/etc/my.cnf</span>，我们定义<span style="background-color: inherit;">/data/mysql/<span style="background-color: inherit;">my.cnf</span></span></span>
        </div>

        <div style="background-color: inherit;">
            <span style="background-color: inherit;">初始化和启动的时候都使用<span style="background-color: inherit;">&nbsp;</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="background-color: inherit;">--defaults-file=<span style="background-color: inherit;">/data/mysql/</span><span style="background-color: inherit;">my.cnf</span><span style="background-color: inherit;">&nbsp;</span></span><span style="background-color: inherit;">参数来指定配置文件</span>
        </div>

            &nbsp;
        </div>

            初始化数据&nbsp;

        <div style="background-color: inherit;">
            <div style="background-color: inherit;">
                &nbsp;<span style="line-height: 1.5; background-color: inherit;">cd&nbsp;</span><span style="line-height: 1.5; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">/usr/local/</span><span style="line-height: 1.5; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">mysql</span>
            </div>

                #<span style="line-height: 1.5; background-color: inherit;">&nbsp;./mysqld&nbsp;--defaults-file=/data/mysql/my.cnf --initialize-insecure</span>

        </div>

        <div style="background-color: inherit;">

                <span style="color: red; font-family: 宋体; background-color: inherit;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 68, 68); font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">在初始化时如果加上<span style="background-color: inherit;">&nbsp;</span></span><span style="color: rgb(153, 51, 0); font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">**&ndash;initial-insecure**</span><span style="color: rgb(68, 68, 68); font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">，</span></span><span style="color: rgb(68, 68, 68); line-height: 1.5; font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">则会</span><span style="color: rgb(68, 68, 68); line-height: 1.5; font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">创建空密码的 root@localhost 账号</span><span style="color: rgb(68, 68, 68); line-height: 1.5; font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">，</span>

                <span style="color: red; font-family: 宋体; background-color: inherit;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 68, 68); font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">否则会创建带密码的 root@localhost 账号，密码直接写在 log-error 日志文件中（在5.6版本中是放在 ~/.mysql_secret 文件里.）</span></span>

        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<div style="font: 14px/21px 微软雅黑; text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); text-transform: none; text-indent: 0px; letter-spacing: normal; word-spacing: 0px; white-space: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">

        启动服务：

    <div style="background-color: inherit;">
        /usr/local/mysql/bin/mysqld_safe&nbsp;--defaults-file=/data/mysql/my.cnf&nbsp;&amp;
    </div>

    <div style="background-color: inherit;">
        &nbsp;
    </div>

        <font color="#444444" face="Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: inherit;"><span style="text-align: left; color: rgb(68, 68, 68); font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">登入</span></font>

    <div style="background-color: inherit;">
        /usr/local/mysql/bin/mysql&nbsp;-S&nbsp;/data/mysql/mysql.sock
    </div>

    <div style="background-color: inherit;">
        设置root密码
    </div>

    <div style="background-color: inherit;">
        <div style="background-color: inherit;">
            mysql&gt;&nbsp;use&nbsp;mysql
        </div>

            mysql&gt;&nbsp;set&nbsp;password&nbsp;=&nbsp;password(&#39;123456&#39;);

    </div>

        mysql&gt;&nbsp;exit

        <span style="font: 14px/21px 微软雅黑; text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); text-transform: none; text-indent: 0px; letter-spacing: normal; word-spacing: 0px; float: none; display: inline !important; white-space: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;">再登入</span>

    <div style="background-color: inherit;">
        <div style="background-color: inherit;">
            /usr/local/mysql/bin/mysql&nbsp;-S&nbsp;/data/mysql/mysql.sock&nbsp;-u&nbsp;root&nbsp;-p
        </div>

            &nbsp;

    </div>

    <div style="background-color: inherit;">
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 微软雅黑; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">

                <span style="color: red; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt; background-color: inherit;">配置允许登陆。</span>

                <span lang="EN-US" style="background-color: inherit;">mysql&gt;use mysql;</span>

        </div>

            <span style="background-color: inherit;"><span lang="EN-US" style="background-color: inherit;">mysql&gt;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="line-height: 1.5; background-color: inherit;">&nbsp;select&nbsp;host,user,authentication_string&nbsp;from&nbsp;user;&nbsp;</span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 1.5; background-color: inherit;">&nbsp;-&nbsp;</span><span style="line-height: 1.5; background-color: inherit;">查看现有用户</span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 1.5; background-color: inherit;">,</span><span style="line-height: 1.5; background-color: inherit;">密码及允许连接的主机 （5.7不同5.6）</span>

            <span style="line-height: 1.5; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">mysql&gt;&nbsp;</span><span style="line-height: 1.5; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">grant&nbsp;all&nbsp;privileges&nbsp;on&nbsp;*.*&nbsp;to&nbsp;root@&#39;localhost&#39;&nbsp;identified&nbsp;by&nbsp;&#39;123456&#39;;<span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">&nbsp;---本地localhost访问 （默认已有）</span></span>

        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 微软雅黑; font-size: 14px; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
            <span lang="EN-US" style="background-color: inherit;">mysql&gt;&nbsp;<span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">grant&nbsp;all&nbsp;privileges&nbsp;on&nbsp;*.*&nbsp;to&nbsp;root@&#39;%&#39;&nbsp;identified&nbsp;by&nbsp;&#39;123456&#39;;</span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;---</span><span style="background-color: inherit;">&lsquo;</span><span lang="EN-US" style="background-color: inherit;">%</span><span style="background-color: inherit;">&rsquo; 任意</span><span lang="EN-US" style="background-color: inherit;">ip</span><span style="background-color: inherit;">访问</span>
        </div>

            <span lang="EN-US" style="background-color: inherit;">mysql&gt;&nbsp;flush privileges;</span>

            <span lang="EN-US" style="background-color: inherit;">mysql&gt;&nbsp;exit</span>

            &nbsp;

    </div>

    <div style="background-color: inherit;">
        关闭服务：
    </div>

    <div style="background-color: inherit;">
        /usr/local/mysql/bin/mysqladmin&nbsp;-S&nbsp;/data/mysql/mysql.sock&nbsp;-u&nbsp;root&nbsp;-p&nbsp;shutdown
    </div>

        &nbsp;

</div>

    &nbsp;
